 133:     """Global FastAPI dependency. None on public paths; raises 401 otherwise.
 134: 
 135:     Phase-0 demo: POLARIS_AUTH_DISABLED=1 short-circuits to None (auth off).
 136:     """
 137:     if os.environ.get("POLARIS_AUTH_DISABLED", "") == "1":
 138:         return None
 139:     if _path_is_public(request.url.path):
 140:         return None
 141:     # Token resolution. Normal routes: Authorization: Bearer header. SSE
 142:     # (/stream/*): the browser's native EventSource cannot set request
 143:     # headers, so the JWT is accepted from the access_token query param —
 144:     # but ONLY for /stream paths, never for state-changing routes.
 145:     token: str | None = None
 146:     if creds is not None and creds.scheme.lower() == "bearer":
 147:         token = creds.credentials
 148:     elif request.url.path.startswith("/stream/"):
 149:         # Trailing slash: only the SSE route /stream/{run_id} — never a
 150:         # lookalike like /streaming/*.
 151:         token = request.query_params.get("access_token")
 152:     if not token:
 153:         raise HTTPException(
 154:             status_code=401,
 155:             detail={"error": "missing_bearer_token", "message": "Authorization: Bearer <jwt> required"},
 156:         )
 157:     try:
 158:         payload = jwt.decode(token, _jwt_secret(), algorithms=[JWT_ALGORITHM])
 159:     except JWTError as exc:
 160:         raise HTTPException(
 161:             status_code=401,
 162:             detail={"error": "invalid_token", "message": str(exc)},
 163:         ) from exc
 164:     return User(username=payload["sub"], role=payload.get("role", "reviewer"))

  20: 
  21: const BACKEND_URL = "/api/v6";
  22: 
  23: /**
  24:  * I-rdy-004 (#500) — fetch wrapper for every v6 API call. Injects the
  25:  * `Authorization: Bearer <jwt>` header, preserves any caller-supplied
  26:  * headers, and does NOT force a content-type (so `FormData` uploads keep
  27:  * their auto-generated multipart boundary). On a 401 it clears the token
  28:  * and routes to /sign-in.
  29:  */
  30: async function authFetch(
  31:   url: string,
  32:   init: RequestInit = {},
  33: ): Promise<Response> {
  34:   const headers = new Headers(init.headers ?? {});
  35:   for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(authHeader())) {
  36:     headers.set(key, value);
  37:   }
  38:   const response = await globalThis.fetch(url, { ...init, headers });
  39:   if (response.status === 401) {
  40:     redirectToSignIn();
  41:   }
  42:   return response;
  43: }
  44: 
  45: /**
  46:  * I-rdy-004 — SSE URL for a run's event stream. Native `EventSource` cannot
  47:  * set request headers, so the JWT rides as the `access_token` query param;
  48:  * the backend `require_auth` accepts it for `/stream/*` paths only.
  49:  */
  50: export function streamUrl(runId: string): string {
  51:   const token = authHeader().Authorization?.replace(/^Bearer /, "");
  52:   const base = `${BACKEND_URL}/stream/${encodeURIComponent(runId)}`;
  53:   return token ? `${base}?access_token=${encodeURIComponent(token)}` : base;

  20: function store(): Storage | null {
  21:   if (typeof window === "undefined") return null;
  22:   return window.sessionStorage;
  23: }
  24: 
  25: /** Current JWT, or null if absent or past its 12h expiry. */
  26: export function getToken(): string | null {
  27:   const s = store();
  28:   if (!s) return null;
  29:   const token = s.getItem(TOKEN_KEY);
  30:   const expiry = s.getItem(EXPIRY_KEY);
  31:   if (!token || !expiry) return null;
  32:   if (Date.now() >= Number(expiry)) {
  33:     clearToken();
  34:     return null;
  35:   }
  36:   return token;
  37: }
  38: 
  39: export function setToken(token: string, expiresInSeconds: number): void {
  40:   const s = store();
  41:   if (!s) return;
  42:   const ttl = expiresInSeconds > 0 ? expiresInSeconds : DEFAULT_EXPIRY_SECONDS;
  43:   s.setItem(TOKEN_KEY, token);
  44:   s.setItem(EXPIRY_KEY, String(Date.now() + ttl * 1000));
  45: }
  46: 
  47: export function clearToken(): void {
  48:   const s = store();
  49:   if (!s) return;
  50:   s.removeItem(TOKEN_KEY);
  51:   s.removeItem(EXPIRY_KEY);
  52: }
  53: 
  54: export function isAuthenticated(): boolean {
  55:   return getToken() !== null;
  56: }
  57: 
  58: /**
  59:  * POST credentials to the backend. On 200, store the JWT and report ok.
  60:  * A 401 here is invalid-credentials feedback for the sign-in form — it is
  61:  * NOT routed through the generic 401-redirect (that would loop the page).
  62:  */
  63: export async function login(
  64:   username: string,
  65:   password: string,
  66: ): Promise<LoginResult> {
  67:   let response: Response;
  68:   try {
  69:     response = await fetch("/api/v6/auth/login", {
  70:       method: "POST",
  71:       headers: { "content-type": "application/json" },
  72:       body: JSON.stringify({ username, password }),
  73:     });
  74:   } catch {
  75:     return { ok: false, status: 0, error: "Could not reach POLARIS. Check the connection." };
  76:   }
  77:   if (response.status === 200) {
  78:     const body = (await response.json()) as {
  79:       access_token: string;
  80:       expires_in?: number;
  81:     };
  82:     setToken(body.access_token, body.expires_in ?? DEFAULT_EXPIRY_SECONDS);
  83:     return { ok: true, status: 200 };
  84:   }
  85:   if (response.status === 401) {
  86:     return { ok: false, status: 401, error: "Invalid username or password." };
  87:   }
  88:   return {
  89:     ok: false,
  90:     status: response.status,
  91:     error: `Sign-in failed (HTTP ${response.status}).`,
  92:   };
  93: }
  94: 
  95: /** Authorization header for the current token, or {} if unauthenticated. */
  96: export function authHeader(): Record<string, string> {
  97:   const token = getToken();
  98:   return token ? { Authorization: `Bearer ${token}` } : {};
  99: }

 104:   clearToken();
